<div class="fp-thumbnail">

<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="#" title=""></a> </h3>
<p>
</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="fp-slides-items">
<div class="fp-thumbnail">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Geoengineering"><img src="wp-content/themes/CarsLine/images/default-slides/3.jpg"/></a> </div>
<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Geoengineering">Geoengineering</a> </h3>
<p>
                                                Geoengineering is the artificial modification of Earths climate systems through two primary ideologies, Solar Radiation Management (SRM) and Carbon Dioxide Removal (CDR) 
                                                
                                                                                            </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="fp-slides-items">
<div class="fp-thumbnail">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Carbon Dioxide Removal (CDR)"><img src="wp-content/themes/CarsLine/images/default-slides/4.jpg"/></a> </div>
<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Carbon Dioxide Removal (CDR)">Carbon Dioxide Removal (CDR)</a> </h3>
<p>
                                                Carbon Dioxide Removal (CDR) and seqeustration. This is artificial trees, ocean fertilization etc. These projects are declassified for the most part. This method of geoengineering IS NOT the focus of this website. 
                                                
                                                                                            </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="fp-slides-items">
<div class="fp-thumbnail">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Solar Radiation Management (SRM)"><img src="wp-content/themes/CarsLine/images/default-slides/6.jpg"/></a> </div>
<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Solar Radiation Management (SRM)">Solar Radiation Management (SRM)</a> </h3>
<p>
                                                Solar Radiation Management (SRM), controlling sunlight before it reaches the planet.  
                                                
                                                                                            </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="fp-slides-items">
<div class="fp-thumbnail">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Stratospheric Sulfate Aerosols Geoengineering (SAG-SRM)"><img src="wp-content/themes/CarsLine/images/default-slides/5.jpg"/></a> </div>
<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Stratospheric Sulfate Aerosols Geoengineering (SAG-SRM)">Stratospheric Sulfate Aerosols Geoengineering (SAG-SRM)</a> </h3>
<p>
                                                The ability of stratospheric sulfate aerosols to create a global dimming effect has made them a possible candidate for use in geoengineering projects to limit the effect and impact ofclimate change due to rising levels of greenhouse gases. Delivery of precursor sulfide gases such as hydrogen sulfide (H2S) or sulfur dioxide (SO2) by artillery, aircraft and balloons has been proposed.  (click image for more...) 
                                                
                                                                                            </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="fp-slides-items">
<div class="fp-thumbnail">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Chemtrailing"><img src="wp-content/themes/CarsLine/images/default-slides/7.jpg"/></a> </div>
<div class="fp-content-wrap">
<div class="fp-content">
<h3 class="fp-title">
<a href="/?page_id=1331" title="Chemtrailing">Chemtrailing</a> </h3>
<p>
                                                Chemtrailing is the publics term for the CLASSIFIED ONGOING artificial modification of Earths climate systems using reflective nano-materials (aerosols) to reflect sunlight. The aerosols are dispersed via jet aircraft trails that expand into reflective artificial clouds. 
                                                
                                                                                            </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<p>
<em><strong>There are several live presentations on the subject of climate engineering available on the windows below. <strong>Click To Open Each Presentation / Video</strong>

<p>
<!-- The Dimming, Full Length Climate Engineering Documentary BEGIN -->

<script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
  jQuery.extend(jQuery.easing, {
      easeOutCubic: function (x, t, b, c, d) {
          return c * ((t = t / d - 1) * t * t + 1) + b;
      }
  });
  jQuery(document).ready(function () {
      var isopen = false,
          bitHeight = jQuery('#bitsubscribe').height();
      setTimeout(function () {
          jQuery('#bit').animate({
              bottom: '-' + bitHeight - 30 + 'px'
          }, 200);
      }, 300);
      jQuery('#bit a.bsub').click(function () {
          if (!isopen) {
              isopen = true;
              jQuery('#bit a.bsub').addClass('open');
              jQuery('#bit #bitsubscribe').addClass('open')
              jQuery('#bit').stop();
              jQuery('#bit').animate({
                  bottom: '0px'
              }, {
                  duration: 400,
                  easing: "easeOutCubic"
              });
          } else {
              isopen = false;
              jQuery('#bit').stop();
              jQuery('#bit').animate({
                  bottom: '-' + bitHeight - 30 + 'px'
              }, 200, function () {
                  jQuery('#bit a.bsub').removeClass('open');
                  jQuery('#bit #bitsubscribe').removeClass('open');
              });
          }
      });
  });
</script>
